Vector2 \mbox{\hyperlink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_ae0c9ecbdb41e04ba3a87b6ffb91cc0a1}{Physics\+Position\+Inheritance\+Factor}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily  \mbox{[}get, set\mbox{]}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em When set to non-\/zero, Transform position movement in X and Y direction is applied to skeleton Physics\+Constraints, multiplied by this scale factor. Typical values are {\ttfamily Vector2.\+one} to apply XY movement 1\+:1, {\ttfamily Vector2(2f, 2f)} to apply movement with double intensity, {\ttfamily Vector2(1f, 0f)} to apply only horizontal movement, or {\ttfamily Vector2.\+zero} to not apply any Transform position movement at all. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
float \mbox{\hyperlink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_a54a44e0c6873572e2e8ded8154435aef}{Physics\+Rotation\+Inheritance\+Factor}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily  \mbox{[}get, set\mbox{]}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em When set to non-\/zero, Transform rotation movement is applied to skeleton Physics\+Constraints, multiplied by this scale factor. Typical values are {\ttfamily 1} to apply movement 1\+:1, {\ttfamily 2} to apply movement with double intensity, or {\ttfamily 0} to not apply any Transform rotation movement at all. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_ab3671b78ebcdbea78dd65ef6b162722e} 
delegate void Spine.\+Unity.\+Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Mesh\+Assignment\+Delegate\+Multiple (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{mesh\+Count}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_spine_a67af89d777151a1d991718c9aaef2332a710fdb6adb881b408116ef95335e1961}{Mesh}}\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}}]{meshes}{, }\item[{Material\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}}]{graphic\+Materials}{, }\item[{Texture\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}}]{textures}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em mesh\+Count} & Number of meshes. Don\textquotesingle{}t use {\ttfamily meshes.\+Length} as this might be higher due to pre-\/allocated entries.\\
\hline
{\em meshes} & Mesh array where each element is normally assigned to one of the {\ttfamily canvas\+Renderers}.\\
\hline
{\em graphic\+Materials} & Material array where each element is normally assigned to one of the {\ttfamily canvas\+Renderers}.\\
\hline
{\em textures} & Texture array where each element is normally assigned to one of the {\ttfamily canvas\+Renderers}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

delegate void Spine.\+Unity.\+Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Mesh\+Assignment\+Delegate\+Single (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_spine_a67af89d777151a1d991718c9aaef2332a710fdb6adb881b408116ef95335e1961}{Mesh}}}]{mesh}{, }\item[{Material}]{graphic\+Material}{, }\item[{Texture}]{texture}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Delegate type for overriding mesh and material assignment, used when {\ttfamily allow\+Multiple\+Canvas\+Renderers} is false. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em mesh} & Mesh normally assigned at the main Canvas\+Renderer.\\
\hline
{\em graphic\+Material} & Material normally assigned at the main Canvas\+Renderer.\\
\hline
{\em texture} & Texture normally assigned at the main Canvas\+Renderer.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Update mode used when the Mesh\+Renderer becomes invisible (when {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_a3c5c24a44e55b02441dc0bb3f9402056}{On\+Became\+Invisible()}} is called). Update mode is automatically reset to {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity_aed56bc8c8f78565588cfcf5fb5998081a6d52930efc1d9c5bdf5424d98f7cd0dd}{Update\+Mode.\+Full\+Update}} when the mesh becomes visible again.

\Hypertarget{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_ae0c9ecbdb41e04ba3a87b6ffb91cc0a1}\index{Spine.Unity.SkeletonGraphic@{Spine.Unity.SkeletonGraphic}!PhysicsPositionInheritanceFactor@{PhysicsPositionInheritanceFactor}}
\index{PhysicsPositionInheritanceFactor@{PhysicsPositionInheritanceFactor}!Spine.Unity.SkeletonGraphic@{Spine.Unity.SkeletonGraphic}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PhysicsPositionInheritanceFactor}{PhysicsPositionInheritanceFactor}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_ae0c9ecbdb41e04ba3a87b6ffb91cc0a1} 
Vector2 Spine.\+Unity.\+Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Physics\+Position\+Inheritance\+Factor\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [get]}, {\ttfamily [set]}}



When set to non-\/zero, Transform position movement in X and Y direction is applied to skeleton Physics\+Constraints, multiplied by this scale factor. Typical values are {\ttfamily Vector2.\+one} to apply XY movement 1\+:1, {\ttfamily Vector2(2f, 2f)} to apply movement with double intensity, {\ttfamily Vector2(1f, 0f)} to apply only horizontal movement, or {\ttfamily Vector2.\+zero} to not apply any Transform position movement at all. 



\mbox{\hyperlink{_skeleton_graphic_8cs_source}{Skeleton\+Graphic.\+cs}} 파일의 \mbox{\hyperlink{_skeleton_graphic_8cs_source_l00592}{592}} 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PhysicsRotationInheritanceFactor}{PhysicsRotationInheritanceFactor}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_a54a44e0c6873572e2e8ded8154435aef} 
float Spine.\+Unity.\+Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Physics\+Rotation\+Inheritance\+Factor\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [get]}, {\ttfamily [set]}}



When set to non-\/zero, Transform rotation movement is applied to skeleton Physics\+Constraints, multiplied by this scale factor. Typical values are {\ttfamily 1} to apply movement 1\+:1, {\ttfamily 2} to apply movement with double intensity, or {\ttfamily 0} to not apply any Transform rotation movement at all.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_a343cc7bbd52877a62d3e203a830796de} 
bool Spine.\+Unity.\+Skeleton\+Graphic.\+Unscaled\+Time\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [get]}, {\ttfamily [set]}}



If enabled, \doxylink{class_spine_1_1_animation_state}{Animation\+State} time is advanced by Unscaled Game Time ({\ttfamily Time.\+unscaled\+Delta\+Time} instead of the default Game Time({\ttfamily Time.\+delta\+Time}). to animate independent of game {\ttfamily Time.\+time\+Scale}. Instance \doxylink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_aa8a9bcd14f230f50926463504690de4b}{Skeleton\+Graphic.\+time\+Scale} and \doxylink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_animation_a835661d8d02afc2f6ff8e9fff371bdf7}{Skeleton\+Animation.\+time\+Scale} will still be applied.

\Hypertarget{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_a78be472079825d470f223e37120e5c45}\index{Spine.Unity.SkeletonGraphic@{Spine.Unity.SkeletonGraphic}!OnMeshAndMaterialsUpdated@{OnMeshAndMaterialsUpdated}}
\index{OnMeshAndMaterialsUpdated@{OnMeshAndMaterialsUpdated}!Spine.Unity.SkeletonGraphic@{Spine.Unity.SkeletonGraphic}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{OnMeshAndMaterialsUpdated}{OnMeshAndMaterialsUpdated}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_a78be472079825d470f223e37120e5c45} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_a92bea5d846f681927b16959e33652a8b}{Skeleton\+Renderer\+Delegate}} Spine.\+Unity.\+Skeleton\+Graphic.\+On\+Mesh\+And\+Materials\+Updated}



On\+Mesh\+And\+Materials\+Updated is raised at the end of {\ttfamily Rebuild} after the Mesh and all materials have been updated. Note that some \doxylink{namespace_spine_1_1_unity}{Unity} API calls are not permitted to be issued from {\ttfamily Rebuild}, so you may want to subscribe to \doxylink{class_spine_1_1_unity_1_1_skeleton_graphic_aeb293ae28959d33b0b9709218d26793a}{On\+Instructions\+Prepared} instead from where you can issue such preparation calls.
